CREATE INDEX  ss2_idx1c ON  #ss2 (siid, series)



--SELECT * FROM #ss2 ORDER BY series ASC;

CREATE TABLE #ss23
    ( areasymbol VARCHAR (15), 
	muname VARCHAR (240),
    mukey INT,
    cokey INT, 
	compname VARCHAR (240),
	comppct_r INT, 
	taxorder VARCHAR (254),
	hzname VARCHAR (40), 
	hzdept_r SMALLINT,
	hzdepb_r SMALLINT,
	ph1to1h2o_r  FLOAT,

	);

----Gets the dominant Component (If more thean 1 component with the same name the script will sum up the component name
----Gets the horizon for 25 CM AND pH 1:1 H20 is greater the 6.5
---TRUNCATE TABLE #ss23
INSERT INTO #ss23

SELECT areasymbol, muname, 
mapunit.mukey,
component.cokey,
CASE WHEN compname LIKE '%variant%' THEN UPPER (REPLACE (compname, 'variant', ''))
	 WHEN compname LIKE '%family%' THEN UPPER (REPLACE (compname, 'family', ''))
	 WHEN compname LIKE '%taxadjunct%' THEN UPPER (REPLACE (compname, 'taxadjunct', '')) ELSE UPPER (REPLACE (compname, '''', '_')) END AS compname, 
comppct_r, 
taxorder,
hzname, 
hzdept_r,
hzdepb_r,
ph1to1h2o_r 
FROM (legend INNER JOIN (mapunit INNER JOIN component ON mapunit.mukey = component.mukey AND majcompflag = 'yes') ON legend.lkey = mapunit.lkey AND  (legend.areasymbol) <> 'US' 
AND component.cokey = 
(SELECT TOP 1 c1.cokey FROM component AS c1 
INNER JOIN mapunit AS c ON c1.mukey=c.mukey AND c.mukey=mapunit.mukey ORDER BY 
SUM(c1.comppct_r) over(partition by compname) DESC , CASE WHEN LEFT (muname,2)= LEFT (compname,2) THEN 1 ELSE 2 END ASC, c1.cokey))
INNER JOIN chorizon ON chorizon.cokey=component.cokey AND 25 BETWEEN hzdept_r AND hzdepb_r AND ph1to1h2o_r >=6.5
ORDER BY muname ASC, compname ASC, component.cokey;


SELECT *
FROM #ss2 
INNER JOIN #ss23 ON #ss23.compname=#ss2.series;
